16. While giving directions you say right / left maaro aur waahan pe ek bridge girega.ğŸ˜‰

17. If Borivali passenger gets into a Virar fast train, that's a *serious crime* boss. ğŸ˜³ğŸ”«

18. Once you survive in a Mumbai local during journey from VT to Kalyan or vice versa during peak hours, you can survive anywhere in the world. ğŸ˜

19. Train timings (7.27, 8.49 etc) are really important events of life.â˜ğŸ»

20. In every local train journey you will find at least one person asking _"arey yeh platform kis taraf aayega?"_ğŸ˜…

21. No salsa, hiphop, moon walk, B'boying or jazz can beat our visarjan dance. ğŸ’ƒğŸ¼ğŸ•ºğŸ»

22. No Starbucks Coffee can beat off our *cutting chai.* â˜•ğŸ˜

23. Nobody remains *"untouched"* once you enter Virar / Karjat fast local. ğŸš…

24. 99% fast trains halt at Goregaon station, but still not indicated...ğŸ˜

25. We dont understand "humko and tumko". We prefer *"tereko and mereko"* ğŸ¤£

26. Second class ticket Rs 10 and first class ticket Rs 110. No difference. You can't sit in either. ğŸ˜†

27. Getting a Virar fast trainğŸš… from Andheri / Borivali during peak hours is more difficult than getting admission into IIT and IIM.ğŸ™ƒ

28. Aur yahan Mumbai mein ghadiâŒš sab ke pas hai, lekin time kisi ke pas nahi hai.
